I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.17495597*A**2 + 0.59132419*sin(log(A + 1))`

Note: `_t = 3.379845758334442` is a fixed constant, so `c2*_t = 0.17495597 * 3.37984576 ‚âà 0.59132419`. The GT has no actual `t` dependence (since `_t` is a fixed constant).

The GT consists of two basis functions:
1. `A¬≤` (polynomial)
2. `sin(log(A + 1))` (transcendental)

The `sin(log(A+1))` term is crucial - it's a very specific transcendental function that cannot be replicated by polynomials, rational functions, exponentials, or simple logarithms.

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidates 2, 3, 6, 11, 30, 41:** These are rational functions (polynomials + terms like `A/(A+c)`). Rational functions cannot produce `sin(log(A+1))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 8, 18, 19, 22, 37, 39, 44:** These have `A¬≤`, `A`, constants, and `exp(c*t)/A^5`. Setting `t`-dependent and `1/A^5` terms to zero leaves polynomials. Cannot produce `sin(log(A+1))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 1, 4, 5, 9, 28, 35, 36:** These involve `log(...)` terms but not `sin(log(...))`. Logarithms are linearly independent from `sin(log(...))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 13, 17, 24, 25, 34, 42:** These involve power functions `A^c` or exponentials. Cannot produce `sin(log(A+1))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 10, 26, 38:** These use `Max(0,A)` which equals `A` for `A‚â•0`, but still only have polynomial/rational/power terms. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** `A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*|A|+1) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*(c6*log(c7*|A|+1))^c8)`. The exponential of a power of log is not `sin(log(...))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** `A¬≤*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7) + c8*exp(c9*t)/A^5`

- `c8 = 0` (eliminate `exp(c9*t)/A^5` term)

This gives: `-0.17495597*A¬≤ + 0.59132419*sin(log(A+1))` ‚úì
